```
Videos that have rotation metadata embedded will by default be rotated when re-encoded in order to produce a video with the correct orientation.
This means you should not try to detect rotation metadata and apply the correction yourself, because it will be done automatically.
```

    20	export const makeVideoTrackHandler =
    21	        ({
    22	                state,
    23	                onVideoFrame,
    24	                onMediaStateUpdate,
    25	                abortConversion,
    26	                controller,
    27	                defaultVideoCodec,

    60	                        resizeOperation,

    64	                const videoOperation = await (onVideoTrack ?? defaultOnVideoTrackHandler)({

    68	                        logLevel,

    70	                        rotate,
    71	                        inputContainer,

    73	                        resizeOperation,
    74	                });

    78	                }
    79

    83	                        );
    84	                }
    85	
    86	                if (videoOperation.type === 'copy') {

    89	                                onMediaStateUpdate,
    90	                                state,
    91	                                track,
    92	                                progressTracker,

     1	import type {MediaParserVideoTrack} from '@remotion/media-parser';
     2	import {isSafari} from './browser-quirks';
     3	import type {ConvertMediaOnVideoFrame} from './convert-media';
     4	import {convertToCorrectVideoFrame} from './convert-to-correct-videoframe';
     5	import type {ConvertMediaVideoCodec} from './get-available-video-codecs';
     6	import type {ResizeOperation} from './resizing/mode';
     7	import {rotateAndResizeVideoFrame} from './rotate-and-resize-video-frame';
     8	
     9	export const onFrame = async ({
    10	        frame: unrotatedFrame,
    11	        onVideoFrame,
    12	        track,
    13	        outputCodec,
    14	        rotation,
    15	        resizeOperation,
    16	}: {
    17	        frame: VideoFrame;
    18	        onVideoFrame: ConvertMediaOnVideoFrame | null;
    19	        track: MediaParserVideoTrack;
    20	        outputCodec: ConvertMediaVideoCodec;
    21	        rotation: number;
    22	        resizeOperation: ResizeOperation | null;
    23	}) => {
    24	        const rotated = rotateAndResizeVideoFrame({
    25	                rotation,
    26	                frame: unrotatedFrame,
    27	                resizeOperation,
    28	                needsToBeMultipleOfTwo: outputCodec === 'h264',
    29	        });
    30	        if (unrotatedFrame !== rotated) {
    31	                unrotatedFrame.close();
    32	        }
    33	
    34	        const userProcessedFrame = onVideoFrame
    35	                ? await onVideoFrame({frame: rotated, track})
    36	                : rotated;
    37	
    38	        if (userProcessedFrame.displayWidth !== rotated.displayWidth) {
    39	                throw new Error(
    40	                        `Returned VideoFrame of track ${track.trackId} has different displayWidth (${userProcessedFrame.displayWidth}) than the input frame (${rotated.displayWidth})`,
    41	                );
    42	        }
    43	
    44	        if (userProcessedFrame.displayHeight !== rotated.displayHeight) {
    45	                throw new Error(
    46	                        `Returned VideoFrame of track ${track.trackId} has different displayHeight (${userProcessedFrame.displayHeight}) than the input frame (${rotated.displayHeight})`,
    47	                );
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        // In Safari, calling new VideoFrame() might change the timestamp
    51	        // In flipVideo test from 803000 to 803299
    52	        if (userProcessedFrame.timestamp !== rotated.timestamp && !isSafari()) {
    53	                throw new Error(
    54	                        `Returned VideoFrame of track ${track.trackId} has different timestamp (${userProcessedFrame.timestamp}) than the input frame (${rotated.timestamp}). When calling new VideoFrame(), pass {timestamp: frame.timestamp} as second argument`,
    55	                );
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        if ((userProcessedFrame.duration ?? 0) !== (rotated.duration ?? 0)) {
    59	                throw new Error(
    60	                        `Returned VideoFrame of track ${track.trackId} has different duration (${userProcessedFrame.duration}) than the input frame (${rotated.duration}). When calling new VideoFrame(), pass {duration: frame.duration} as second argument`,
    61	                );
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        if (rotated !== userProcessedFrame) {
    65	                rotated.close();
    66	        }
    67	
    68	        const fixedFrame = convertToCorrectVideoFrame({
    69	                videoFrame: userProcessedFrame,
    70	                outputCodec,
    71	        });
    72	        if (fixedFrame !== userProcessedFrame) {
    73	                userProcessedFrame.close();
    74	        }
    75	
    76	        return fixedFrame;
    77	};
    78

     1	import type {MediaParserDimensions} from '@remotion/media-parser';
     2	import {calculateNewSizeAfterResizing} from './resizing/calculate-new-size';
     3	import type {ResizeOperation} from './resizing/mode';
     4	import {normalizeVideoRotation} from './rotate-and-resize-video-frame';
     5	
     6	export const calculateNewDimensionsFromRotate = ({
     7	        height,
     8	        width,
     9	        rotation,
    10	}: MediaParserDimensions & {
    11	        rotation: number;
    12	}) => {
    13	        const normalized = normalizeVideoRotation(rotation);
    14	        const switchDimensions = normalized % 90 === 0 && normalized % 180 !== 0;
    15	
    16	        const newHeight = switchDimensions ? width : height;
    17	        const newWidth = switchDimensions ? height : width;
    18	        return {
    19	                height: newHeight,
    20	                width: newWidth,
    21	        };
    22	};
    23	
    24	export const calculateNewDimensionsFromRotateAndScale = ({
    25	        width,
    26	        height,
    27	        rotation,
    28	        resizeOperation,
    29	        needsToBeMultipleOfTwo,
    30	}: {
    31	        width: number;
    32	        height: number;
    33	        rotation: number;
    34	        resizeOperation: ResizeOperation | null;
    35	        needsToBeMultipleOfTwo: boolean;
    36	}) => {
    37	        const {height: newHeight, width: newWidth} = calculateNewDimensionsFromRotate(
    38	                {
    39	                        height,
    40	                        rotation,
    41	                        width,
    42	                },
    43	        );
    44	
    45	        return calculateNewSizeAfterResizing({
    46	                dimensions: {height: newHeight, width: newWidth},
    47	                resizeOperation,
    48	                needsToBeMultipleOfTwo,
    49	        });
    50	};
    51

     1	import type {ResizeOperation} from './resizing/mode';
     2	import {
     3	        calculateNewDimensionsFromRotate,
     4	        calculateNewDimensionsFromRotateAndScale,
     5	} from './rotation';
     6	
     7	export const normalizeVideoRotation = (rotation: number) => {
     8	        return ((rotation % 360) + 360) % 360;
     9	};
    10	
    11	export const rotateAndResizeVideoFrame = ({
    12	        frame,
    13	        rotation,
    14	        needsToBeMultipleOfTwo = false,
    15	        resizeOperation,
    16	}: {
    17	        frame: VideoFrame;
    18	        rotation: number;
    19	        resizeOperation: ResizeOperation | null;
    20	        needsToBeMultipleOfTwo?: boolean;
    21	}) => {
    22	        const normalized = normalizeVideoRotation(rotation);
    23	
    24	        // No resize, no rotation
    25	        if (normalized === 0 && resizeOperation === null) {
    26	                return frame;
    27	        }
    28	
    29	        if (normalized % 90 !== 0) {
    30	                throw new Error('Only 90 degree rotations are supported');
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        const {height, width} = calculateNewDimensionsFromRotateAndScale({
    34	                height: frame.displayHeight,
    35	                width: frame.displayWidth,
    36	                rotation,
    37	                needsToBeMultipleOfTwo,
    38	                resizeOperation,
    39	        });
    40	
    41	        // No rotation, and resize turned out to be same dimensions
    42	        if (
    43	                normalized === 0 &&
    44	                height === frame.displayHeight &&
    45	                width === frame.displayWidth
    46	        ) {
    47	                return frame;
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        const canvas = new OffscreenCanvas(width, height);
    51	        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    52	        if (!ctx) {
    53	                throw new Error('Could not get 2d context');
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        canvas.width = width;
    57	        canvas.height = height;
    58	
    59	        // @ts-expect-error
    60	        const frameRotation: number = frame.rotation ?? 0;
    61	        const canvasRotationToApply = normalizeVideoRotation(
    62	                normalized + frameRotation,
    63	        );
    64	
    65	        if (canvasRotationToApply === 90) {
    66	                ctx.translate(width, 0);
    67	        } else if (canvasRotationToApply === 180) {
    68	                ctx.translate(width, height);
    69	        } else if (canvasRotationToApply === 270) {
    70	                ctx.translate(0, height);
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        if (canvasRotationToApply !== 0) {
    74	                ctx.rotate(canvasRotationToApply * (Math.PI / 180));
    75	        }
    76	
    77	        if (frame.displayHeight !== height || frame.displayWidth !== width) {
    78	                const dimensionsAfterRotate = calculateNewDimensionsFromRotate({
    79	                        height: frame.displayHeight,
    80	                        rotation,
    81	                        width: frame.displayWidth,
    82	                });
    83	                ctx.scale(
    84	                        width / dimensionsAfterRotate.width,
    85	                        height / dimensionsAfterRotate.height,
    86	                );
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        ctx.drawImage(frame, 0, 0);
    90	
    91	        return new VideoFrame(canvas, {
    92	                displayHeight: height,
    93	                displayWidth: width,
    94	                duration: frame.duration ?? undefined,
    95	                timestamp: frame.timestamp,
    96	        });
    97	};
    98

   123	export const getNumberOfTracks = (moovBox: MoovBox): number => {
   124	        const mvHdBox = getMvhdBox(moovBox);
   125	        if (!mvHdBox) {

   146	export const getHasTracks = (
   147	        state: ParserState,
   148	        mayUsePrecomputed: boolean,
   149	): boolean => {
   150	        const structure = state.structure.getStructure();
   151	        if (structure.type === 'matroska') {
   152	                return matroskaHasTracks({
   153	                        structureState: state.structure,
   154	                        webmState: state.webm,
   155	                });
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        if (structure.type === 'iso-base-media') {
   159	                return isoBaseMediaHasTracks(state, mayUsePrecomputed);
   160	        }
   161	
   162	        if (structure.type === 'riff') {
   163	                return hasAllTracksFromAvi(state);
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        if (structure.type === 'transport-stream') {
   167	                return hasAllTracksFromTransportStream(state);
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        if (structure.type === 'mp3') {
   171	                return state.callbacks.tracks.getTracks().length > 0;
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        if (structure.type === 'wav') {
   175	                return state.callbacks.tracks.hasAllTracks();
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        if (structure.type === 'aac') {
   179	                return state.callbacks.tracks.hasAllTracks();
   180	        }
   181	
   182	        if (structure.type === 'flac') {
   183	                return state.callbacks.tracks.hasAllTracks();
   184	        }
   185	
   186	        if (structure.type === 'm3u') {
   187	                return state.callbacks.tracks.hasAllTracks();
   188	        }
   189	
   190	        throw new Error('Unknown container ' + (structure satisfies never));
   191	};

   193	const getCategorizedTracksFromMatroska = (
   194	        state: ParserState,
   195	): MediaParserTrack[] => {
   196	        const {resolved} = getTracksFromMatroska({
   197	                structureState: state.structure,
   198	                webmState: state.webm,
   199	        });
   200	
   201	        return resolved;
   202	};
   203	
   204	export const getTracksFromMoovBox = (moovBox: MoovBox): MediaParserTrack[] => {
   205	        const mediaParserTracks: MediaParserTrack[] = [];
   206	        const tracks = getTraks(moovBox);
   207	
   208	        for (const trakBox of tracks) {
   209	                const mvhdBox = getMvhdBox(moovBox);
   210	                if (!mvhdBox) {
   211	                        throw new Error('Mvhd box is not found');
   212	                }
   213	
   214	                const startTime = findTrackStartTimeInSeconds({
   215	                        movieTimeScale: mvhdBox.timeScale,
   216	                        trakBox,
   217	                });
   218	                const track = makeBaseMediaTrack(trakBox, startTime);
   219	                if (!track) {
   220	                        continue;
   221	                }
   222	
   223	                mediaParserTracks.push(track);
   224	        }
   225	
   226	        return mediaParserTracks;
   227	};
   228	
   229	export const getTracksFromIsoBaseMedia = ({
   230	        mayUsePrecomputed,
   231	        structure,
   232	        isoState,
   233	        m3uPlaylistContext,
   234	}: {
   235	        structure: StructureState;
   236	        isoState: IsoBaseMediaState;
   237	        m3uPlaylistContext: M3uPlaylistContext | null;
   238	        mayUsePrecomputed: boolean;
   239	}): MediaParserTrack[] => {
   240	        const moovBox = getMoovBoxFromState({
   241	                structureState: structure,
   242	                isoState,
   243	                mp4HeaderSegment: m3uPlaylistContext?.mp4HeaderSegment ?? null,
   244	                mayUsePrecomputed,
   245	        });
   246	        if (!moovBox) {
   247	                return [];
   248	        }
   249	
   250	        return getTracksFromMoovBox(moovBox);
   251	};
   252	
   253	export const defaultGetTracks = (
   254	        parserState: ParserState,
   255	): MediaParserTrack[] => {
   256	        const tracks = parserState.callbacks.tracks.getTracks();
   257	        if (tracks.length === 0) {
   258	                throw new Error('No tracks found');
   259	        }
   260	
   261	        return tracks;
   262	};
   263	
   264	export const defaultHasallTracks = (parserState: ParserState): boolean => {
   265	        try {
   266	                defaultGetTracks(parserState);
   267	                return true;
   268	        } catch {
   269	                return false;
   270	        }
   271	};
   272	
   273	export const getTracks = (
   274	        state: ParserState,
   275	        mayUsePrecomputed: boolean,
   276	): MediaParserTrack[] => {
   277	        const structure = state.structure.getStructure();
   278	        if (structure.type === 'matroska') {
   279	                return getCategorizedTracksFromMatroska(state);
   280	        }
   281	
   282	        if (structure.type === 'iso-base-media') {
   283	                return getTracksFromIsoBaseMedia({
   284	                        isoState: state.iso,
   285	                        m3uPlaylistContext: state.m3uPlaylistContext,
   286	                        structure: state.structure,
   287	                        mayUsePrecomputed,
   288	                });
   289	        }
   290	
   291	        if (structure.type === 'riff') {
   292	                return getTracksFromAvi(structure, state);
   293	        }
   294	
   295	        if (structure.type === 'transport-stream') {
   296	                return getTracksFromTransportStream(state);
   297	        }
   298	
   299	        if (
   300	                structure.type === 'mp3' ||
   301	                structure.type === 'wav' ||
   302	                structure.type === 'flac' ||
   303	                structure.type === 'aac' ||
   304	                structure.type === 'm3u'
   305	        ) {
   306	                return defaultGetTracks(state);
   307	        }
   308	
   309	        throw new Error(`Unknown container${structure satisfies never}`);
   310	};

     1	import {MediaParserInternals} from '@remotion/media-parser';
     2	import {canReencodeVideoTrack} from './can-reencode-video-track';
     3	import type {
     4	        ConvertMediaOnVideoTrackHandler,
     5	        VideoOperation,
     6	} from './on-video-track-handler';
     7	
     8	export const defaultOnVideoTrackHandler: ConvertMediaOnVideoTrackHandler =
     9	        async ({
    10	                track,
    11	                defaultVideoCodec,
    12	                logLevel,
    13	                rotate,
    14	                canCopyTrack,
    15	                resizeOperation,
    16	        }): Promise<VideoOperation> => {
    17	                if (canCopyTrack) {
    18	                        MediaParserInternals.Log.verbose(
    19	                                logLevel,
    20	                                `Track ${track.trackId} (video): Can copy, therefore copying`,
    21	                        );
    22	
    23	                        return Promise.resolve({type: 'copy'});
    24	                }
    25	
    26	                if (defaultVideoCodec === null) {
    27	                        MediaParserInternals.Log.verbose(
    28	                                logLevel,
    29	                                `Track ${track.trackId} (video): Is audio container, therefore dropping video`,
    30	                        );
    31	                        return Promise.resolve({type: 'drop'});
    32	                }
    33	
    34	                const canReencode = await canReencodeVideoTrack({
    35	                        videoCodec: defaultVideoCodec,
    36	                        track,
    37	                        resizeOperation,
    38	                        rotate,
    39	                });
    40	
    41	                if (canReencode) {
    42	                        MediaParserInternals.Log.verbose(
    43	                                logLevel,
    44	                                `Track ${track.trackId} (video): Cannot copy, but re-enconde, therefore re-encoding`,
    45	                        );
    46	
    47	                        return Promise.resolve({
    48	                                type: 'reencode',
    49	                                videoCodec: defaultVideoCodec,
    50	                                rotate: rotate - track.rotation,
    51	                                resize: resizeOperation,
    52	                        });
    53	                }
    54	
    55	                MediaParserInternals.Log.verbose(
    56	                        logLevel,
    57	                        `Track ${track.trackId} (video): Can neither copy nor re-encode, therefore failing`,
    58	                );
    59	
    60	                return Promise.resolve({type: 'fail'});
    61	        };

     8	import type {ResizeOperation} from './resizing/mode';
     9	import {normalizeVideoRotation} from './rotate-and-resize-video-frame';
    10	import {calculateNewDimensionsFromRotateAndScale} from './rotation';
    11	
    12	export const canCopyVideoTrack = ({
    13	        outputContainer,
    14	        rotationToApply,
    15	        inputContainer,
    16	        resizeOperation,
    17	        inputTrack,
    18	        outputVideoCodec,
    19	}: {
    20	        inputContainer: MediaParserContainer;
    21	        inputTrack: MediaParserVideoTrack;
    22	        rotationToApply: number;
    23	        outputContainer: ConvertMediaContainer;
    24	        outputVideoCodec: ConvertMediaVideoCodec | null;
    25	        resizeOperation: ResizeOperation | null;
    26	}) => {

    28	                normalizeVideoRotation(inputTrack.rotation) !==
    29	                normalizeVideoRotation(rotationToApply)
    30	        ) {
    31	                return false;
    32	        }
    33	
    34	        if (outputVideoCodec) {
    35	                if (
    36	                        !isSameVideoCodec({
    37	                                inputVideoCodec: inputTrack.codecEnum,
    38	                                outputCodec: outputVideoCodec,
    39	                        })
    40	                ) {
    41	                        return false;
    42	                }
    43	        }
    44	
    45	        const needsToBeMultipleOfTwo = inputTrack.codecEnum === 'h264';
    46	
    47	        const newDimensions = calculateNewDimensionsFromRotateAndScale({
    48	                height: inputTrack.height,
    49	                resizeOperation,
    50	                rotation: rotationToApply,
    51	                width: inputTrack.width,
    52	                needsToBeMultipleOfTwo,
    53	        });
    54	        if (
    55	                newDimensions.height !== inputTrack.height ||
    56	                newDimensions.width !== inputTrack.width
    57	        ) {
    58	                return false;
    59	        }
    60	
    61	        if (outputContainer === 'webm') {
    62	                return inputTrack.codecEnum === 'vp8' || inputTrack.codecEnum === 'vp9';
    63	        }
    64	
    65	        if (outputContainer === 'mp4') {
    66	                return (
    67	                        (inputTrack.codecEnum === 'h264' || inputTrack.codecEnum === 'h265') &&
    68	                        (inputContainer === 'mp4' ||
    69	                                inputContainer === 'avi' ||
    70	                                (inputContainer === 'm3u8' && inputTrack.m3uStreamFormat === 'mp4'))
    71	                );
    72	        }
    73	
    74	        if (outputContainer === 'wav') {

2025-12-27 18:20:34,344 - INFO - swea-agent - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

     1	import type {ResizeOperation} from './resizing/mode';
     2	import {
     3		calculateNewDimensionsFromRotate,
     4		calculateNewDimensionsFromRotateAndScale,
     5	} from './rotation';
     6	
     7	export const normalizeVideoRotation = (rotation: number) => {
     8		return ((rotation % 360) + 360) % 360;
     9	};
    10	
    11	export const rotateAndResizeVideoFrame = ({
    12		frame,
    13		rotation,
    14		needsToBeMultipleOfTwo = false,
    15		resizeOperation,
    16	}: {
    17		frame: VideoFrame;
    18		rotation: number;
    19		resizeOperation: ResizeOperation | null;
    20		needsToBeMultipleOfTwo?: boolean;
    21	}) => {
    22		const normalized = normalizeVideoRotation(rotation);
    23	
    24		// No resize, no rotation
    25		if (normalized === 0 && resizeOperation === null) {
    26			return frame;
    27		}
    28	
    29		if (normalized % 90 !== 0) {
    30			throw new Error('Only 90 degree rotations are supported');
    31		}
    32	
    33		const {height, width} = calculateNewDimensionsFromRotateAndScale({
    34			height: frame.displayHeight,
    35			width: frame.displayWidth,
    36			rotation,
    37			needsToBeMultipleOfTwo,
    38			resizeOperation,
    39		});
    40	
    41		// No rotation, and resize turned out to be same dimensions
    42		if (
    43			normalized === 0 &&
    44			height === frame.displayHeight &&
    45			width === frame.displayWidth
    46		) {
    47			return frame;
    48		}
    49	
    50		const canvas = new OffscreenCanvas(width, height);
    51		const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    52		if (!ctx) {
    53			throw new Error('Could not get 2d context');
    54		}
    55	
    56		canvas.width = width;
    57		canvas.height = height;
    58	
    59		// @ts-expect-error
    60		const frameRotation: number = frame.rotation ?? 0;
    61		const canvasRotationToApply = normalizeVideoRotation(
    62			normalized + frameRotation,
    63		);
    64	
    65		if (canvasRotationToApply === 90) {
    66			ctx.translate(width, 0);
    67		} else if (canvasRotationToApply === 180) {
    68			ctx.translate(width, height);
    69		} else if (canvasRotationToApply === 270) {
    70			ctx.translate(0, height);
    71		}
    72	
    73		if (canvasRotationToApply !== 0) {
    74			ctx.rotate(canvasRotationToApply * (Math.PI / 180));
    75		}
    76	
    77		if (frame.displayHeight !== height || frame.displayWidth !== width) {
    78			const dimensionsAfterRotate = calculateNewDimensionsFromRotate({
    79				height: frame.displayHeight,
    80				rotation,
    81				width: frame.displayWidth,
    82			});
    83			ctx.scale(
    84				width / dimensionsAfterRotate.width,
    85				height / dimensionsAfterRotate.height,
    86			);
    87		}
    88	
    89		ctx.drawImage(frame, 0, 0);
    90	
    91		return new VideoFrame(canvas, {
    92			displayHeight: height,
    93			displayWidth: width,
    94			duration: frame.duration ?? undefined,
    95			timestamp: frame.timestamp,
    96		});
    97	};

    12	export const canCopyVideoTrack = ({

+                videoDecoder.decode(chunk);
+        };

+        };

+        async ({
+                track,
+                defaultVideoCodec,
+                logLevel,
+                rotate,
+                canCopyTrack,
+                resizeOperation,
+        }): Promise<VideoOperation> => {
+                if (canCopyTrack) {
+                        MediaParserInternals.Log.verbose(
+                                logLevel,
+                                `Track ${track.trackId} (video): Can copy, therefore copying`,
+                        );
+
+                        return Promise.resolve({type: 'copy'});
+                }
+
+                if (defaultVideoCodec === null) {
+                        MediaParserInternals.Log.verbose(
+                                logLevel,
+                                `Track ${track.trackId} (video): Is audio container, therefore dropping video`,
+                        );
+                        return Promise.resolve({type: 'drop'});
+                }
+
+                const canReencode = await canReencodeVideoTrack({
+                        videoCodec: defaultVideoCodec,
+                        track,
+                        resizeOperation,
+                        rotate,
+                });
+
+                if (canReencode) {
+                        MediaParserInternals.Log.verbose(
+                                logLevel,
+                                `Track ${track.trackId} (video): Cannot copy, but re-enconde, therefore re-encoding`,
+                        );
+
+                        return Promise.resolve({
+                                type: 'reencode',
+                                videoCodec: defaultVideoCodec,
+                                rotate: rotate,
+                                resize: resizeOperation,
+                        });
+                }
+
+                MediaParserInternals.Log.verbose(
+                        logLevel,
+                        `Track ${track.trackId} (video): Can neither copy nor re-encode, therefore failing`,
+                );
+
+                return Promise.resolve({type: 'fail'});
+        };

+                await getVideoDecoderConfigWithHardwareAcceleration(track);

+        Log.verbose(logLevel, 'Video encoder config', videoEncoderConfig);

+                abortConversion(
+                        new Error(`Could not configure video decoder of track ${track.trackId}`),
+                );
+                return null;
+        }
+
+        const {trackNumber} = await state.addTrack({
+                type: 'video',
+                color: track.advancedColor,
+                width: newWidth,
+                height: newHeight,
+                codec: videoOperation.videoCodec,
+                codecPrivate: null,
+                timescale: track.originalTimescale,

+        Log.verbose(
+                logLevel,
+                `Created new video track with ID ${trackNumber}, codec ${videoOperation.videoCodec} and timescale ${track.originalTimescale}`,
+        );

+        const videoEncoder = createVideoEncoder({
+                onChunk: async (chunk, metadata) => {
+                        await state.addSample({
+                                chunk: convertEncodedChunk(chunk),
+                                trackNumber,
+                                isVideo: true,
+                                codecPrivate: arrayBufferToUint8Array(
+                                        (metadata?.decoderConfig?.description ?? null) as ArrayBuffer | null,
+                                ),
+                        });
+                        onMediaStateUpdate?.((prevState) => {
+                                return {
+                                        ...prevState,
+                                        encodedVideoFrames: prevState.encodedVideoFrames + 1,
+                                };
+                        });
+                },
+                onError: (err) => {
+                        abortConversion(
+                                new Error(
+                                        `Video encoder of track ${track.trackId} failed (see .cause of this error)`,
+                                        {
+                                                cause: err,
+                                        },
+                                ),
+                        );
+                },
+                controller,
+                config: videoEncoderConfig,
+                logLevel,
+                outputCodec: videoOperation.videoCodec,
+                keyframeInterval: 40,
+        });
+
+        const videoProcessingQueue = processingQueue<VideoFrame>({
+                controller,
+                label: 'VideoFrame processing queue',
+                logLevel,
+                onError: (err) => {
+                        abortConversion(
+                                new Error(
+                                        `VideoFrame processing queue of track ${track.trackId} failed (see .cause of this error)`,
+                                        {
+                                                cause: err,
+                                        },
+                                ),
+                        );
+                },
+                onOutput: async (frame) => {
+                        await controller._internals._mediaParserController._internals.checkForAbortAndPause();
+
+                        const processedFrame = await onFrame({
+                                frame,
+                                track,
+                                onVideoFrame,
+                                outputCodec: videoOperation.videoCodec,
+                                rotation,
+                                resizeOperation: videoOperation.resize ?? null,
+                        });
+
+                        await controller._internals._mediaParserController._internals.checkForAbortAndPause();
+                        await videoEncoder.ioSynchronizer.waitForQueueSize(10);
+
+                        await controller._internals._mediaParserController._internals.checkForAbortAndPause();
+                        videoEncoder.encode(processedFrame);
+
+                        processedFrame.close();
+                },
+        });
+
+        const frameSorter = videoFrameSorter({
+                controller,
+                onOutput: async (frame) => {
+                        await controller._internals._mediaParserController._internals.checkForAbortAndPause();
+                        await videoProcessingQueue.ioSynchronizer.waitForQueueSize(10);
+
+                        videoProcessingQueue.input(frame);
+                },
+        });
+
+        const videoDecoder = createVideoDecoder({
+                track: videoDecoderConfig,
+                onFrame: async (frame) => {
+                        await frameSorter.waitUntilProcessed();
+                        frameSorter.inputFrame(frame);
+                },
+                onError: (err) => {
+                        abortConversion(
+                                new Error(
+                                        `Video decoder of track ${track.trackId} failed (see .cause of this error)`,
+                                        {
+                                                cause: err,
+                                        },
+                                ),
+                        );
+                },
+                controller,
+                logLevel,
+        });
+
+        state.addWaitForFinishPromise(async () => {
+                Log.verbose(logLevel, 'Waiting for video decoder to finish');
+                await videoDecoder.flush();
+                videoDecoder.close();
+                Log.verbose(
+                        logLevel,
+                        'Video decoder finished. Waiting for encoder to finish',
+                );
+
+                await frameSorter.flush();
+                Log.verbose(logLevel, 'Frame sorter flushed');
+
+                await videoProcessingQueue.ioSynchronizer.waitForQueueSize(0);
+                Log.verbose(logLevel, 'Video processing queue finished');
+
+                await videoEncoder.waitForFinish();
+                videoEncoder.close();
+                Log.verbose(logLevel, 'Video encoder finished');
+        });
+
+        return async (chunk) => {
+                progressTracker.setPossibleLowestTimestamp(
+                        Math.min(chunk.timestamp, chunk.decodingTimestamp ?? Infinity),
+                );
+
+                await controller._internals._mediaParserController._internals.checkForAbortAndPause();
+                await videoDecoder.waitForQueueToBeLessThan(15);
+
+                if (chunk.type === 'key') {
+                        await videoDecoder.flush();
+                }
+
+                videoDecoder.decode(chunk);
+        };
 };
